# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 Header Normalization Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that handle HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 header translation: the header case normalization (lowercase), the pseudo-header injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority), and the upgrade header handling.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

- **Role**: Core HTTP/1.1 codec interface definition

- **Role**: HTTP/1.1 codec implementation
- **Key Functions**:
  - `onHeadersComplete()` - Called when headers are fully parsed
  - `decodeHeaders()` - Decodes HTTP/1.1 headers
  - `encodeHeaders()` - Encodes headers for HTTP/1.1
- **Responsibilities**:
  - Pseudo-header injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority)
  - Header translation from HTTP/1.1 format
  - Connection upgrade handling

### 3. **source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.h**
- **Role**: Header formatting utilities
- **Responsibilities**:
  - Header case normalization
  - Case conversion logic

### 4. **source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc**
- **Role**: Implementation of header formatting
- **Functions**:
  - Lowercase conversion utilities
  - Header normalization functions
- **Responsibilities**:
  - Converting header names to lowercase
  - Header formatting for HTTP/2

Perfect! I've successfully created a comprehensive analysis of the C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that handle HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 header translation. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Findings

**Files Identified (11 total)**:
1. **codec_impl.cc/h** - Core header translation with pseudo-header injection and normalization
2. **balsa_parser.cc/h** - HTTP/1.1 parser
3. **header_formatter.cc/h** - Header case formatting
4. **header_map_impl.cc/h** - Header storage and retrieval
5. **headers.h** - Pseudo-header definitions
6. **header_utility.cc/h** - Header utilities

**Key Mechanisms**:

1. **Header Case Normalization** (source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc, line 568):
   - All header names are converted to lowercase using `inlineTransform()`
   - Occurs in `ConnectionImpl::completeCurrentHeader()`

2. **Pseudo-Header Injection** (source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc):
   - `:method` - Extracted from request line (line 1233)
   - `:path` - Extracted from request URI (line 1174)
   - `:scheme` - Extracted from URL scheme (line 1160)
   - `:authority` - Set from Host header or URL (line 1156)

3. **Upgrade Header Handling** (source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc, lines 855-885):
   - Detects and processes HTTP/2 Cleartext (h2c)
   - Handles CONNECT method as upgrade
   - Processes WebSocket and other upgrades

This is essential for HTTP/2 compliance, as all header names in HTTP/2 MUST be lowercase per RFC 7540.\\n\\n## Pseudo-Header Injection\\n\\nPseudo-headers are injected during header processing in **source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc** in the `ServerConnectionImpl::onHeadersCompleteBase()` function (lines 1201-1266):\\n\\n1. **:method** (line 1233):\\n   - `headers->setMethod(parser_->methodName());`\\n   - Extracted from the HTTP/1.1 request line (GET, POST, CONNECT, etc.)\\n   - Set directly as a pseudo-header\\n\\n2. **:path** (line 1174 in handlePath):\\n   - `headers.setPath(absolute_url.pathAndQueryParams());`\\n   - Extracted from the request-target in the request line\\n   - Handles both absolute-form and origin-form URLs\\n\\n3. **:scheme** (line 1160 in handlePath):\\n   - `headers.setScheme(absl::AsciiStrToLower(absolute_url.scheme()));`\\n   - Extracted from absolute-form URLs or inferred from connection type (http/https)\\n   - Lowercased for HTTP/2 compliance\\n\\n4. **:authority** (line 1156 in handlePath):\\n   - `headers.setHost(absolute_url.hostAndPort());`\\n   - Set from the absolute-form URL's host and port or from the Host header\\n   - Replaces or validates the Host header as per RFC 7230\\n\\n## Upgrade Header Handling\\n\\nUpgrade header processing occurs in **source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc** in `ConnectionImpl::onHeadersCompleteImpl()` (lines 855-885):\\n\\n- Detects Upgrade and Connection headers\\n- Handles HTTP/2 Cleartext (h2c) upgrade requests (currently removed)\\n- Processes WebSocket and other upgrade requests\\n- Sets the `handling_upgrade_` flag to enter upgrade mode\\n- Special handling for CONNECT method (treated as upgrade)\\n\\n## Processing Pipeline\\n\\n### 1. Parsing Phase\\n**source/common/http/http1/balsa_parser.cc**:\\n- `BalsaParser::execute()` - Main parsing entry point\\n- `BalsaParser::OnRequestFirstLineInput()` - Parses request line (method, URI, version)\\n- `BalsaParser::validateAndProcessHeadersOrTrailersImpl()` - Processes individual headers\\n- Validates header names and values according to RFC specifications\\n\\n### 2. Header Field/Value Accumulation\\n**source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc**:\\n- `ConnectionImpl::onHeaderFieldImpl()` - Accumulates header field name\\n- `ConnectionImpl::onHeaderValueImpl()` - Accumulates header field value\\n- Handles whitespace trimming per RFC 7230\\n\\n### 3. Header Completion and Normalization\\n**source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc**, `ConnectionImpl::completeCurrentHeader()`:\\n- Applies stateful formatter for header case preservation (if configured)\\n- Normalizes header name to lowercase using `inlineTransform()`\\n- Validates header name contains no underscore characters (if required)\\n- Adds header to the header map via `addViaMove()`\\n\\n### 4. Header Map Storage\\n**source/common/http/header_map_impl.cc**:\\n- `HeaderMapImpl::addReferenceKey()` - Adds header with lowercase key\\n- Headers are stored with `LowerCaseString` keys for case-insensitive lookup\\n- Pseudo-headers are distinguished by leading colon in the name\\n\\n### 5. Pseudo-Header Finalization\\n**source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc**, `ServerConnectionImpl::onHeadersCompleteBase()`:\\n- Handles URL parsing and scheme validation\\n- Injects :method, :path, :scheme, :authority pseudo-headers\\n- Validates that the resulting header set is valid for HTTP/2\\n- Calls `HeaderUtility::requestHeadersValid()` to verify RFC compliance\\n\\n## Header Formatter Integration\\n\\n**source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc** and **source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.h**:\\n- Provides `ProperCaseHeaderKeyFormatter` for optional header case formatting\\n- Allows Envoy to preserve or format header names during encoding\\n- Applied during stateful formatting in `completeCurrentHeader()` (line 566)\\n- The formatter is called with the original header name before lowercasing\\n\\n## Key Constants and Definitions\\n\\n**source/common/http/headers.h**:\\n- Defines pseudo-header names: `:method`, `:path`, `:scheme`, `:authority`, `:protocol`\\n- Defines standard HTTP/1.1 headers and their HTTP/2 equivalents\\n- Method values (GET, POST, CONNECT, HEAD, etc.)\\n- Scheme values (http, https)\\n\\n## Connection Upgrade Detection\\n\\nUpgrade handling in **source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc** (lines 855-885):\\n- Checks for Upgrade and Connection headers\\n- Detects h2c (HTTP/2 Cleartext) and other upgrade types\\n- For h2c: removes unsupported upgrade headers\\n- For CONNECT: automatically enters upgrade mode\\n- Uses helper function `caseUnorderedSetContainingUpgradeAndHttp2Settings()` for case-insensitive header comparison\\n\\nThis comprehensive header translation system ensures that HTTP/1.1 requests are properly converted to HTTP/2-compliant headers with all required pseudo-headers, proper case normalization, and correct upgrade handling.\"\n}\n",
